     1	﻿using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
     2	using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Web;
     3	using MudBlazor.Utilities;
     4	
     5	namespace MudBlazor
     6	{
     7	    /// <summary>
     8	    /// A component for collecting start and end values which define a range.
     9	    /// </summary>
    10	    /// <typeparam name="T">The type of object managed by this input.</typeparam>
    11	    public partial class MudRangeInput<T> : MudBaseInput<Range<T>>
    12	    {
    13	        private string? _textStart;
    14	        private string? _textEnd;
    15	        private ElementReference _elementReferenceStart;
    16	        private ElementReference _elementReferenceEnd;
    17	
    18	        /// <summary>
    19	        /// Creates a new instance.
    20	        /// </summary>
    21	        public MudRangeInput()
    22	        {
    23	            Value = new Range<T>();
    24	        }
    25	
    26	        protected string Classname => MudInputCssHelper.GetClassname(this,
    27	            () => !string.IsNullOrEmpty(ReadText)
    28	                  || Adornment == Adornment.Start
    29	                  || !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(PlaceholderStart)
    30	                  || !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(PlaceholderEnd)
    31	                  || ShrinkLabel);
    32	
    33	        protected internal override InputType GetInputType() => InputType;
    34	
    35	        protected string InputClassname => MudInputCssHelper.GetInputClassname(this);
    36	
    37	        protected string AdornmentClassname => MudInputCssHelper.GetAdornmentClassname(this);
    38	
    39	        protected string ClearButtonClassname =>
    40	            new CssBuilder("mud-input-clear-button")
    41	                .AddClass(Adornment is Adornment.Start ? "me-0" : "me-n4")
    42	                .Build();
    43	
    44	        /// <summary>
    45	        /// The type of input collected by this component.
    46	        /// </summary>
    47	        /// <remarks>
    48	        /// Defaults to <see cref="InputType.Text"/>.  Represents a valid HTML5 input type.
    49	        /// </remarks>
    50	        [Parameter]
    51	        public InputType InputType { get; set; } = InputType.Text;
    52	
    53	        /// <summary>
    54	        /// The hint displayed before the user enters a starting value.
    55	        /// </summary>
    56	        [Parameter]
    57	        public string? PlaceholderStart { get; set; }
    58	
    59	        /// <summary>
    60	        /// The hint displayed before the user enters an ending value.
    61	        /// </summary>
    62	        [Parameter]
    63	        public string? PlaceholderEnd { get; set; }
    64	
    65	        /// <summary>
    66	        /// Occurs when the Clear button is clicked.
    67	        /// </summary>
    68	        /// <remarks>
    69	        /// When clicked, the <see cref="MudBaseInput{T}.Text"/> and <see cref="MudBaseInput{T}.Value"/> properties are reset.
    70	        /// </remarks>
    71	        [Parameter]
    72	        public EventCallback<MouseEventArgs> OnClearButtonClick { get; set; }
    73	
    74	        /// <summary>
    75	        /// Shows a button at the end of the input to clear the value.
    76	        /// </summary>
    77	        /// <remarks>
    78	        /// Defaults to <c>false</c>.
    79	        /// When <c>true</c>, an icon is displayed which, when clicked, clears the Text and Value.  Use the <see cref="ClearIcon"/> property to control the Clear button icon.
    80	        /// </remarks>
    81	        [Parameter]
    82	        public bool Clearable { get; set; }
    83	
    84	        /// <summary>

   113	        /// Moves the cursor to the starting input component.
   114	        /// </summary>
   115	        public ValueTask FocusStartAsync() => _elementReferenceStart.FocusAsync();
   116	
   117	        public override async ValueTask BlurAsync()
   118	        {
   119	            await _elementReferenceStart.MudBlurAsync();
   120	            await _elementReferenceEnd.MudBlurAsync();
   121	        }
   122	
   123	        /// <summary>
   124	        /// Selects the text in the starting input.
   125	        /// </summary>
   126	        public ValueTask SelectStartAsync() => _elementReferenceStart.MudSelectAsync();
   127	
   128	        /// <summary>
   129	        /// Selects the text in the start value.
   130	        /// </summary>
   131	        /// <param name="pos1">The index of the first character to select.</param>
   132	        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
   133	        public ValueTask SelectRangeStartAsync(int pos1, int pos2) => _elementReferenceStart.MudSelectRangeAsync(pos1, pos2);
   134	
   135	        /// <summary>
   136	        /// Moves the cursor to the ending input component.
   137	        /// </summary>
   138	        public ValueTask FocusEndAsync() => _elementReferenceEnd.FocusAsync();
   139	
   140	        /// <summary>
   141	        /// Selects the text in the ending input.
   142	        /// </summary>
   143	        public ValueTask SelectEndAsync() => _elementReferenceEnd.MudSelectAsync();
   144	
   145	        /// <summary>
   146	        /// Selects the text in the end value.
   147	        /// </summary>
   148	        /// <param name="pos1">The index of the first character to select.</param>
   149	        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
   150	        public ValueTask SelectRangeEndAsync(int pos1, int pos2) => _elementReferenceEnd.MudSelectRangeAsync(pos1, pos2);
   151	
   152	        /// <summary>
   153	        /// The text of the start of the range.
   154	        /// </summary>
   155	        public string? TextStart
   156	        {
   157	            get => _textStart;
   158	            set
   159	            {
   160	                if (_textStart == value)
   161	                    return;
   162	                _textStart = value;
   163	                SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(RangeUtility.Join(_textStart, _textEnd)).CatchAndLog();
   164	            }
   165	        }
   166	
   167	        /// <summary>
   168	        /// The text of the end of the range.
   169	        /// </summary>
   170	        public string? TextEnd
   171	        {
   172	            get => _textEnd;
   173	            set
   174	            {
   175	                if (_textEnd == value)
   176	                    return;
   177	                _textEnd = value;
   178	                SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(RangeUtility.Join(_textStart, _textEnd)).CatchAndLog();
   179	            }
   180	        }
   181	
   182	        protected string InputTypeString => InputType.ToStringFast(true);
   183	
   184	        protected bool IsClearable() => Clearable && ReadValue is not null;
   185	
   186	        /// <inheritdoc />
   187	        protected override IConverter<Range<T>?, string?> GetDefaultConverter()
   188	        {
   189	            return new RangeConverter<T>
   190	            {
   191	                Culture = GetCulture,
   192	                Format = GetFormat
   193	            };
   194	        }
   195	
   196	        protected override async Task UpdateTextPropertyAsync(bool updateValue)
   197	        {
   198	            await base.UpdateTextPropertyAsync(updateValue);
   199	
   200	            RangeUtility.Split(ReadText, out _textStart, out _textEnd);
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        protected override async Task UpdateValuePropertyAsync(bool updateText)
   204	        {
   205	            await base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync(updateText);
   206	
   207	            RangeUtility.Split(ReadText, out _textStart, out _textEnd);
   208	        }
   209	
   210	        protected virtual async Task ClearButtonClickHandlerAsync(MouseEventArgs e)
   211	        {
   212	            await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(string.Empty, updateValue: true);
   213	            await _elementReferenceStart.FocusAsync();
   214	            await OnClearButtonClick.InvokeAsync(e);
   215	        }
   216	    }
   217	}

   112	        /// </summary>

   116	        [Parameter]

   118	        public bool AllowDisabledDatesInRange { get; set; } = false;
   119	
   120	        protected async Task SetDateRangeAsync(DateRange? range, bool updateValue)
   121	        {
   122	            // Normalize the DateRange before exception is thrown
   123	            range = NormalizeDateRange(range);
   124	
   125	            if (_dateRange != range)
   126	            {
   127	                var doesRangeContainDisabledDates = !AllowDisabledDatesInRange && range is { Start: not null, End: not null } && Enumerable
   128	                    .Range(0, int.MaxValue)
   129	                    .Select(index => range.Start.Value.AddDays(index))
   130	                    .TakeWhile(date => date <= range.End.Value)
   131	                    .Any(date => IsDateDisabledFunc(date.Date));
   132	
   133	                if (doesRangeContainDisabledDates)
   134	                {
   135	                    _rangeText = null;
   136	                    await SetTextAsync(null, false);
   137	                    return;
   138	                }
   139	
   140	                Touched = true;
   141	
   142	                if (range?.Start is not null && StartMonth == null)
   143	                    PickerMonth = new DateTime(GetCulture().Calendar.GetYear(range.Start.Value), GetCulture().Calendar.GetMonth(range.Start.Value), 1, GetCulture().Calendar);
   144	
   145	                _dateRange = range;
   146	                _value = range?.End;
   147	                HighlightedDate = range?.Start;
   148	
   149	                if (updateValue)
   150	                {
   151	                    ResetConverterErrors();
   152	                    if (_dateRange == null || (_dateRange.Start == null && _dateRange.End == null))
   153	                    {
   154	                        _rangeText = null;
   155	                        await SetTextAsync(null, false);
   156	                    }
   157	                    else
   158	                    {
   159	                        _rangeText = new Range<string>(
   160	                            ConvertSet(_dateRange.Start),
   161	                            ConvertSet(_dateRange.End));
   162	                        await SetTextAsync(_dateRange.ToString(GetConverter()), false);
   163	                    }
   164	                }
   165	
   166	                await DateRangeChanged.InvokeAsync(_dateRange);
   167	                await BeginValidateAsync();
   168	                FieldChanged(_value);
   169	            }
   170	        }
   171	
   172	        private Range<string>? RangeText
   173	        {
   174	            get => _rangeText;
   175	            set
   176	            {
   177	                if (_rangeText?.Equals(value) ?? (value == null))
   178	                    return;
   179	
   180	                Touched = true;
   181	                _rangeText = value;
   182	                SetDateRangeAsync(value is null ? null : ParseDateRangeValue(value.Start, value.End), false).CatchAndLog();
   183	            }
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        private MudRangeInput<string> _rangeInput = null!;
   187

   192

   195	        /// </summary>
   196	        public ValueTask SelectStartAsync() => _rangeInput.SelectStartAsync();
   197	
   198	        /// <summary>
   199	        /// Selects a portion of the start input text.
   200	        /// </summary>
   201	        /// <param name="pos1">The index of the first character to select.</param>
   202	        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
   203	        public ValueTask SelectRangeStartAsync(int pos1, int pos2) => _rangeInput.SelectRangeStartAsync(pos1, pos2);
   204	
   205	        /// <summary>
   206	        /// Focuses the end input.
   207	        /// </summary>
   208	        public ValueTask FocusEndAsync() => _rangeInput.FocusEndAsync();
   209	
   210	        /// <summary>
   211	        /// Selects the end input text.
   212	        /// </summary>
   213	        public ValueTask SelectEndAsync() => _rangeInput.SelectEndAsync();
   214	
   215	        public override ValueTask BlurAsync() => _rangeInput.BlurAsync();
   216	
   217	        /// <summary>
   218	        /// Selects a portion of the end input text.
   219	        /// </summary>
   220	        /// <param name="pos1">The index of the first character to select.</param>
   221	        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
   222	        public ValueTask SelectRangeEndAsync(int pos1, int pos2) => _rangeInput.SelectRangeEndAsync(pos1, pos2);
   223	
   224	        protected override Task DateFormatChangedAsync(string? newFormat)
   225	        {
   226	            Touched = true;
   227	            _rangeText = null;
   228	            if (_dateRange?.Start != null || _dateRange?.End != null)
   229	            {
   230	                _rangeText = new Range<string>(
   231	                    ConvertSet(_dateRange.Start),
   232	                    ConvertSet(_dateRange.End));
   233	            }
   234	
   235	            return SetTextAsync(_dateRange?.ToString(GetConverter()), false);
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        protected override Task StringValueChangedAsync(string? value)
   239	        {
   240	            Touched = true;
   241	            // Update the date range property (without updating back the Value property)
   242	            return SetDateRangeAsync(ParseDateRangeValue(value), false);
   243	        }
   244	
   245	        protected override bool HasValue(DateTime? value) => value is not null;
   246	
   247	        protected override bool IsDayDisabled(DateTime date)
   248	        {
   249	            if (_firstDate is null || _secondDate is not null)
   250	            {
   251	                return base.IsDayDisabled(date);
   252	            }
   253	
   254	            var selectedDate = _firstDate.Value;
   255	            var validDateRange = GetValidDateRange(selectedDate);
   256	
   257	            return base.IsDayDisabled(date) || IsDateOutOfRange(date, selectedDate, validDateRange);
   258	        }
   259	
   260	        private DateRange GetValidDateRange(DateTime selectedDate)
   261	        {
   262	            var start = MinDays switch
   263	            {
   264	                null => MinDate ?? DateTime.MinValue,
   265	                _ when _allowDisabledDatesInCountState.Value => selectedDate.Date.AddDays(MinDays.Value - 1),
   266	                _ => _minValidDate
   267	            };
   268	
   269	            var end = MaxDays switch
   270	            {
   271	                null => MaxDate ?? DateTime.MaxValue,
   272	                _ when _allowDisabledDatesInCountState.Value => selectedDate.Date.AddDays(MaxDays.Value - 1),
   273	                _ => _maxValidDate
   274	            };
   275	
   276	            return new DateRange(start, end);
   277	        }
   278	
   279	        private static bool IsDateOutOfRange(DateTime date, DateTime selectedDate, DateRange validRange)
   280	        {
   281	            var isNotSelectedDate = date < selectedDate || date > selectedDate;
   282	            var isOutsideValidRange = date < validRange.Start || date > validRange.End;
   283	
   284	            return isNotSelectedDate && isOutsideValidRange;
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        private DateTime GetMaxSelectableDate(DateTime startDate, int maxDays)
   288	        {
   289	            var validDayCount = 1;
   290	            var lastValidDate = startDate;
   291	            var maxDate = startDate.AddDays(1);
   292	
   293	            while (validDayCount < maxDays)
   294	            {
   295	                if (!IsDateDisabledFunc(maxDate))
   296	                {
   297	                    validDayCount++;
   298	                    lastValidDate = maxDate;
   299	                }
   300	
   301	                if (validDayCount == maxDays)
   302	                    break;
   303	
   304	                if (maxDate.Date > MaxDate.GetValueOrDefault(startDate.AddYears(50)).Date)
   305	                    break;
   306	
   307	                if (maxDate.Date == DateTime.MaxValue.Date)
   308	                    break;
   309	
   310	                maxDate = maxDate.AddDays(1);
   311	            }
   312	
   313	            return lastValidDate;
   314	        }
   315	
   316	        /// <summary>
   317	        /// Recalculate the valid days in relation to the <see cref="MinDays"/> and <see cref="MaxDays"/> allowed
   318	        /// </summary>
   319	        public void RecalculateValidDays()
   320	        {
   321	            if (_firstDate is null) return;
   322	
   323	            if (MinDays is not null)
   324	                _minValidDate = GetMaxSelectableDate(_firstDate.Value, MinDays.Value);
   325	
   326	            if (MaxDays is not null)
   327	                _maxValidDate = GetMaxSelectableDate(_firstDate.Value, MaxDays.Value);
   328	
   329	            StateHasChanged();
   330	        }
   331	
   332	        private DateRange? ParseDateRangeValue(string? value)
   333	        {
   334	            return DateRange.TryParse(value, GetConverter(), out var dateRange) ? dateRange : null;
   335	        }
   336	
   337	        private DateRange? ParseDateRangeValue(string? start, string? end)
   338	        {
   339	            return DateRange.TryParse(start, end, GetConverter(), out var dateRange) ? dateRange : null;
   340	        }
   341	
   342	        protected override Task OnPickerClosedAsync()
   343	        {
   344	            _firstDate = null;
   345	
   346	            return base.OnPickerClosedAsync();
   347	        }
   348	
   349	        private bool CheckDateRange(DateTime day, Func<DateTime, DateTime, bool> compareStart, Func<DateTime, DateTime, bool> compareEnd)
   350	        {
   351	            return _firstDate is null
   352	                && _dateRange is { Start: { } start, End: { } end }
   353	                && compareStart(start.Date, day)
   354	                && compareEnd(end.Date, day);
   355	        }
   356	
   357	        protected override string GetDayClasses(int month, DateTime day)
   358	        {
   359	            var b = new CssBuilder("mud-day");
   360	            b.AddClass(AdditionalDateClassesFunc?.Invoke(day) ?? string.Empty);
   361	            if (day < GetMonthStart(month) || day > GetMonthEnd(month))
   362	            {
   363	                return b.AddClass("mud-hidden").Build();
   364	            }
   365	
   366	            static bool isLessThan(DateTime date1, DateTime date2) => date1 < date2;
   367	            static bool isGreaterThan(DateTime date1, DateTime date2) => date1 > date2;
   368	            static bool isEqualTo(DateTime date1, DateTime date2) => date1 == date2;
   369	            static bool isNotEqualTo(DateTime date1, DateTime date2) => date1 != date2;
   370	
   371	            if ((_firstDate?.Date < day && _secondDate?.Date > day) || CheckDateRange(day, compareStart: isLessThan, compareEnd: isGreaterThan))
   372	            {
   373	                return b
   374	                    .AddClass("mud-range")
   375	                    .AddClass("mud-range-between")
   376	                    .AddClass($"mud-current mud-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}-text mud-button-outlined mud-button-outlined-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}", day == DateTime.Today)
   377	                    .Build();
   378	            }
   379	
   380	            if (_firstDate?.Date == day && _secondDate?.Date == day)
   381	            {
   382	                return b.AddClass("mud-selected")
   383	                    .AddClass($"mud-theme-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}")
   384	                    .Build();
   385	            }
   386	
   387	            if (_firstDate?.Date == day || CheckDateRange(day, compareStart: isEqualTo, compareEnd: isNotEqualTo))
   388	            {
   389	                return b.AddClass("mud-selected")
   390	                    .AddClass("mud-range")
   391	                    .AddClass("mud-range-start-selected")
   392	                    .AddClass("mud-range-selection", _firstDate != null)
   393	                    .AddClass($"mud-theme-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}")
   394	                    .Build();
   395	            }
   396	
   397	            if ((_firstDate is { } && _secondDate?.Date == day) || CheckDateRange(day, compareStart: isNotEqualTo, compareEnd: isEqualTo))
   398	            {
   399	                return b.AddClass("mud-selected")
   400	                    .AddClass("mud-range")
   401	                    .AddClass("mud-range-end-selected")
   402	                    .AddClass($"mud-theme-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}")
   403	                    .Build();
   404	            }
   405	
   406	            if (CheckDateRange(day, compareStart: isEqualTo, compareEnd: isEqualTo))
   407	            {
   408	                return b.AddClass("mud-selected").AddClass($"mud-theme-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}").Build();
   409	            }
   410	
   411	            if (_firstDate?.Date < day)
   412	            {
   413	                return b.AddClass("mud-range", _secondDate is null && day != DateTime.Today)
   414	                    .AddClass("mud-range-selection")
   415	                    .AddClass($"mud-range-selection-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}", _firstDate is not null)
   416	                    .AddClass($"mud-current mud-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}-text mud-button-outlined mud-button-outlined-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}", day == DateTime.Today)
   417	                    .Build();
   418	            }
   419	
   420	            if (day == DateTime.Today)
   421	            {
   422	                return b.AddClass("mud-current")
   423	                    .AddClass($"mud-button-outlined mud-button-outlined-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}")
   424	                    .AddClass($"mud-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}-text")
   425	                    .Build();
   426	            }
   427	
   428	            return b.Build();
   429	        }
   430	
   431	        protected override async Task OnDayClickedAsync(DateTime dateTime)
   432	        {
   433	            if (GetReadOnlyState())
   434	                return;
   435	            if (_firstDate == null || _secondDate != null)
   436	            {
   437	                _secondDate = null;
   438	                _firstDate = dateTime;
   439	
   440	                RecalculateValidDays();
   441	
   442	                return;
   443	            }
   444	            if (_firstDate > dateTime)
   445	            {
   446	                _secondDate = _firstDate;
   447	                _firstDate = dateTime;
   448	            }
   449	            else
   450	            {
   451	                _secondDate = dateTime;
   452	            }
   453	            if (PickerActions == null || AutoClose)
   454	            {
   455	                await SubmitAsync();
   456	
   457	                if (PickerVariant != PickerVariant.Static)
   458	                {
   459	                    await Task.Delay(TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(ClosingDelay), TimeProvider);
   460	                    await CloseAsync(false);
   461	                }
   462	            }
   463	        }
   464	
   465	        protected override Task OnOpenedAsync()
   466	        {
   467	            _secondDate = null;
   468	            return base.OnOpenedAsync();
   469	        }
   470	
   471	        protected internal override async Task SubmitAsync()
   472	        {
   473	            if (GetReadOnlyState())
   474	                return;
   475	            if (_firstDate == null || _secondDate == null)
   476	                return;
   477	
   478	            await SetDateRangeAsync(new DateRange(_firstDate, _secondDate), true);
   479	
   480	            _firstDate = null;
   481	            _secondDate = null;
   482	        }
   483	
   484	        protected override Task ResetValueAsync() => ClearAsync();
   485	
   486	        public override async Task ClearAsync(bool close = true)
   487	        {
   488	            await SetDateRangeAsync(null, true);
   489	            _firstDate = _secondDate = null;
   490	            await base.ClearAsync(close);
   491	        }
   492	
   493	        protected override string GetTitleDateString()
   494	        {
   495	            if (_firstDate != null)
   496	                return $"{FormatTitleDate(_firstDate)} - {FormatTitleDate(_secondDate)}";
   497	
   498	            return DateRange?.Start != null
   499	                ? $"{FormatTitleDate(DateRange.Start)} - {FormatTitleDate(DateRange.End)}"
   500	                : "";
   501	        }
   502	
   503	        protected override DateTime GetCalendarStartOfMonth()
   504	        {
   505	            var date = StartMonth ?? DateRange?.Start ?? DateTime.Today;
   506	            return date.StartOfMonth(GetCulture());
   507	        }
   508	
   509	        protected override async Task OnYearClickedAsync(int year)
   510	        {
   511	            await base.OnYearClickedAsync(year);
   512	
   513	            if (DateRange?.Start is null && _firstDate is null)
   514	            {
   515	                HighlightedDate = PickerMonth;
   516	            }
   517	        }
   518	
   519	        protected override int GetCalendarYear(DateTime yearDate)
   520	        {
   521	            var date = DateRange?.Start ?? DateTime.Today;
   522	            var diff = GetCulture().Calendar.GetYear(date) - GetCulture().Calendar.GetYear(yearDate);
   523	            var calenderYear = GetCulture().Calendar.GetYear(date);
   524	            return calenderYear - diff;
   525	        }
   526	
   527	        /// <summary>
   528	        /// Normalize a date by treating DateTime.MinValue as null
   529	        /// This prevents an ArgumentOutOfRangeException from happening when performing date arithmetic
   530	        /// </summary>
   531	        /// <param name="date">The date to normalize</param>
   532	        /// <returns>Normalized date or null</returns>
   533	        private static DateTime? NormalizeDate(DateTime? date)
   534	        {
   535	            if (date is null)
   536	                return null;
   537	
   538	            // Treat DateTime.MinValue as null
   539	            if (date.Value == DateTime.MinValue)
   540	                return null;
   541	
   542	            return date;
   543	        }
   544	
   545	        /// <summary>
   546	        /// Normalize a date range by checking the start date and end date for DateTime.MinValue
   547	        /// This prevents an ArgumentOutOfRangeException from happening when performing date arithmetic
   548	        /// </summary>
   549	        /// <see cref="NormalizeDate"/>
   550	        /// <param name="range">The date range to normalize</param>
   551	        /// <returns>Normalized date range or null</returns>
   552	        private static DateRange? NormalizeDateRange(DateRange? range)
   553	        {
   554	            if (range is null)
   555	                return null;
   556	
   557	            var start = NormalizeDate(range.Start);
   558	            var end = NormalizeDate(range.End);
   559	
   560	            return new DateRange(start, end);
   561	        }
   562	
   563	    }
   564	}

    44	    that the ResXResourceWriter will generate, however the reader can 
    45	    read any of the formats listed below.
    46	    
    47	    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.binary.base64
    48	    value   : The object must be serialized with 
    49	            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Binary.BinaryFormatter
    50	            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    51	    
    52	    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.soap.base64
    53	    value   : The object must be serialized with 
    54	            : System.Runtime.Serialization.Formatters.Soap.SoapFormatter
    55	            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    56	
    57	    mimetype: application/x-microsoft.net.object.bytearray.base64
    58	    value   : The object must be serialized into a byte array 
    59	            : using a System.ComponentModel.TypeConverter
    60	            : and then encoded with base64 encoding.
    61	    -->

   121	        public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }
   122	
   123	        /// <summary>
   124	        /// The icon shown in between start and end values.
   125	        /// </summary>
   126	        /// <remarks>
   127	        /// Defaults to <see cref="Icons.Material.Filled.ArrowRightAlt"/>.
   128	        /// </remarks>
   129	        [Parameter]
   130	        public string SeparatorIcon { get; set; } = Icons.Material.Filled.ArrowRightAlt;
   131	
   132	        /// <summary>
   133	        /// Moves the cursor to the starting input component.
   134	        /// </summary>
   135	        public ValueTask FocusStartAsync() => _elementReferenceStart.FocusAsync();
   136	
   137	        public override async ValueTask BlurAsync()
   138	        {
   139	            await _elementReferenceStart.MudBlurAsync();
   140	            await _elementReferenceEnd.MudBlurAsync();
   141	        }
   142	
   143	        /// <summary>
   144	        /// Selects the text in the starting input.
   145	        /// </summary>
   146	        public ValueTask SelectStartAsync() => _elementReferenceStart.MudSelectAsync();
   147	
   148	        /// <summary>
   149	        /// Selects the text in the start value.
   150	        /// </summary>
   151	        /// <param name="pos1">The index of the first character to select.</param>
   152	        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
   153	        public ValueTask SelectRangeStartAsync(int pos1, int pos2) => _elementReferenceStart.MudSelectRangeAsync(pos1, pos2);
   154	
   155	        /// <summary>
   156	        /// Moves the cursor to the ending input component.
   157	        /// </summary>
   158	        public ValueTask FocusEndAsync() => _elementReferenceEnd.FocusAsync();
   159	
   160	        /// <summary>
   161	        /// Selects the text in the ending input.
   162	        /// </summary>
   163	        public ValueTask SelectEndAsync() => _elementReferenceEnd.MudSelectAsync();
   164	
   165	        /// <summary>
   166	        /// Selects the text in the end value.
   167	        /// </summary>
   168	        /// <param name="pos1">The index of the first character to select.</param>
   169	        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
   170	        public ValueTask SelectRangeEndAsync(int pos1, int pos2) => _elementReferenceEnd.MudSelectRangeAsync(pos1, pos2);
   171	
   172	        /// <summary>
   173	        /// The text of the start of the range.
   174	        /// </summary>
   175	        public string? TextStart
   176	        {
   177	            get => _textStart;
   178	            set
   179	            {
   180	                if (_textStart == value)
   181	                    return;
   182	                _textStart = value;
   183	                SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(RangeUtility.Join(_textStart, _textEnd)).CatchAndLog();
   184	            }
   185	        }
   186	
   187	        /// <summary>
   188	        /// The text of the end of the range.
   189	        /// </summary>
   190	        public string? TextEnd
   191	        {
   192	            get => _textEnd;
   193	            set
   194	            {
   195	                if (_textEnd == value)
   196	                    return;
   197	                _textEnd = value;
   198	                SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(RangeUtility.Join(_textStart, _textEnd)).CatchAndLog();
   199	            }
   200	        }
   201	
   202	        protected string InputTypeString => InputType.ToStringFast(true);
   203	
   204	        protected bool IsClearable() => Clearable && ReadValue is not null;
   205	
   206	        /// <inheritdoc />
   207	        protected override IConverter<Range<T>?, string?> GetDefaultConverter()
   208	        {
   209	            return new RangeConverter<T>
   210	            {
   211	                Culture = GetCulture,
   212	                Format = GetFormat
   213	            };
   214	        }
   215	
   216	        protected override async Task UpdateTextPropertyAsync(bool updateValue)
   217	        {
   218	            await base.UpdateTextPropertyAsync(updateValue);
   219	
   220	            RangeUtility.Split(ReadText, out _textStart, out _textEnd);
   221	        }
   222	
   223	        protected override async Task UpdateValuePropertyAsync(bool updateText)
   224	        {
   225	            await base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync(updateText);
   226	
   227	            RangeUtility.Split(ReadText, out _textStart, out _textEnd);
   228	        }
   229	
   230	        protected virtual async Task ClearButtonClickHandlerAsync(MouseEventArgs e)
   231	        {
   232	            await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(string.Empty, updateValue: true);
   233	            await _elementReferenceStart.FocusAsync();
   234	            await OnClearButtonClick.InvokeAsync(e);
   235	        }
   236	    }
   237	}

﻿using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components;
using Microsoft.AspNetCore.Components.Web;
using MudBlazor.Utilities;

namespace MudBlazor
{
    /// <summary>
    /// A component for collecting start and end values which define a range.
    /// </summary>
    /// <typeparam name="T">The type of object managed by this input.</typeparam>
    public partial class MudRangeInput<T> : MudBaseInput<Range<T>>
    {
        private string? _textStart;
        private string? _textEnd;
        private ElementReference _elementReferenceStart;
        private ElementReference _elementReferenceEnd;

        /// <summary>
        /// Creates a new instance.
        /// </summary>
        public MudRangeInput()
        {
            Value = new Range<T>();
        }

        protected string Classname => MudInputCssHelper.GetClassname(this,
            () => !string.IsNullOrEmpty(ReadText)
                  || Adornment == Adornment.Start
                  || !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(PlaceholderStart)
                  || !string.IsNullOrWhiteSpace(PlaceholderEnd)
                  || ShrinkLabel);

        protected internal override InputType GetInputType() => InputType;

        protected string InputClassname => MudInputCssHelper.GetInputClassname(this);

        protected string AdornmentClassname => MudInputCssHelper.GetAdornmentClassname(this);

        protected string ClearButtonClassname =>
            new CssBuilder("mud-input-clear-button")
                .AddClass(Adornment is Adornment.Start ? "me-0" : "me-n4")
                .Build();

        /// <summary>
        /// The type of input collected by this component.
        /// </summary>
        /// <remarks>
        /// Defaults to <see cref="InputType.Text"/>.  Represents a valid HTML5 input type.
        /// </remarks>
        [Parameter]
        public InputType InputType { get; set; } = InputType.Text;

        /// <summary>
        /// The hint displayed before the user enters a starting value.
        /// </summary>
        [Parameter]
        public string? PlaceholderStart { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// The hint displayed before the user enters an ending value.
        /// </summary>
        [Parameter]
        public string? PlaceholderEnd { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// Occurs when the Clear button is clicked.
        /// </summary>
        /// <remarks>
        /// When clicked, the <see cref="MudBaseInput{T}.Text"/> and <see cref="MudBaseInput{T}.Value"/> properties are reset.
        /// </remarks>
        [Parameter]
        public EventCallback<MouseEventArgs> OnClearButtonClick { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// Shows a button at the end of the input to clear the value.
        /// </summary>
        /// <remarks>
        /// Defaults to <c>false</c>.
        /// When <c>true</c>, an icon is displayed which, when clicked, clears the Text and Value.  Use the <see cref="ClearIcon"/> property to control the Clear button icon.
        /// </remarks>
        [Parameter]
        public bool Clearable { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// Custom clear icon when <see cref="Clearable"/> is enabled.
        /// </summary>
        /// <remarks>
        /// Defaults to <see cref="Icons.Material.Filled.Clear"/>.
        /// </remarks>
        [Parameter]
        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Appearance)]
        public string ClearIcon { get; set; } = Icons.Material.Filled.Clear;

        /// <summary>
        /// The accessible name for the starting input field.
        /// </summary>
        /// <remarks>
        /// Defaults to a localized "Start" label when <c>null</c>.
        /// </remarks>
        [Parameter]
        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Behavior)]
        public string? StartInputAriaLabel { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// The accessible name for the ending input field.
        /// </summary>
        /// <remarks>
        /// Defaults to a localized "End" label when <c>null</c>.
        /// </remarks>
        [Parameter]
        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Behavior)]
        public string? EndInputAriaLabel { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// The content within this input component.
        /// </summary>
        /// <remarks>
        /// Will only display if <see cref="InputType"/> is <see cref="InputType.Hidden"/>.
        /// </remarks>
        [Parameter]
        public RenderFragment? ChildContent { get; set; }

        /// <summary>
        /// The icon shown in between start and end values.
        /// </summary>
        /// <remarks>
        /// Defaults to <see cref="Icons.Material.Filled.ArrowRightAlt"/>.
        /// </remarks>
        [Parameter]
        public string SeparatorIcon { get; set; } = Icons.Material.Filled.ArrowRightAlt;

        /// <summary>
        /// Moves the cursor to the starting input component.
        /// </summary>
        public ValueTask FocusStartAsync() => _elementReferenceStart.FocusAsync();

        public override async ValueTask BlurAsync()
        {
            await _elementReferenceStart.MudBlurAsync();
            await _elementReferenceEnd.MudBlurAsync();
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// Selects the text in the starting input.
        /// </summary>
        public ValueTask SelectStartAsync() => _elementReferenceStart.MudSelectAsync();

        /// <summary>
        /// Selects the text in the start value.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="pos1">The index of the first character to select.</param>
        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
        public ValueTask SelectRangeStartAsync(int pos1, int pos2) => _elementReferenceStart.MudSelectRangeAsync(pos1, pos2);

        /// <summary>
        /// Moves the cursor to the ending input component.
        /// </summary>
        public ValueTask FocusEndAsync() => _elementReferenceEnd.FocusAsync();

        /// <summary>
        /// Selects the text in the ending input.
        /// </summary>
        public ValueTask SelectEndAsync() => _elementReferenceEnd.MudSelectAsync();

        /// <summary>
        /// Selects the text in the end value.
        /// </summary>
        /// <param name="pos1">The index of the first character to select.</param>
        /// <param name="pos2">The index of the last character to select.</param>
        public ValueTask SelectRangeEndAsync(int pos1, int pos2) => _elementReferenceEnd.MudSelectRangeAsync(pos1, pos2);

        /// <summary>
        /// The text of the start of the range.
        /// </summary>
        public string? TextStart
        {
            get => _textStart;
            set
            {
                if (_textStart == value)
                    return;
                _textStart = value;
                SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(RangeUtility.Join(_textStart, _textEnd)).CatchAndLog();
            }
        }

        /// <summary>
        /// The text of the end of the range.
        /// </summary>
        public string? TextEnd
        {
            get => _textEnd;
            set
            {
                if (_textEnd == value)
                    return;
                _textEnd = value;
                SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(RangeUtility.Join(_textStart, _textEnd)).CatchAndLog();
            }
        }

        protected string InputTypeString => InputType.ToStringFast(true);

        protected bool IsClearable() => Clearable && ReadValue is not null;

        /// <inheritdoc />
        protected override IConverter<Range<T>?, string?> GetDefaultConverter()
        {
            return new RangeConverter<T>
            {
                Culture = GetCulture,
                Format = GetFormat
            };
        }

        protected override async Task UpdateTextPropertyAsync(bool updateValue)
        {
            await base.UpdateTextPropertyAsync(updateValue);

            RangeUtility.Split(ReadText, out _textStart, out _textEnd);
        }

        protected override async Task UpdateValuePropertyAsync(bool updateText)
        {
            await base.UpdateValuePropertyAsync(updateText);

            RangeUtility.Split(ReadText, out _textStart, out _textEnd);
        }

        protected virtual async Task ClearButtonClickHandlerAsync(MouseEventArgs e)
        {
            await SetTextAndUpdateValueAsync(string.Empty, updateValue: true);
            await _elementReferenceStart.FocusAsync();
            await OnClearButtonClick.InvokeAsync(e);
        }
    }
}

   102	        [Parameter]
   103	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Data)]
   104	        public DateRange? DateRange
   105	        {

   110	        /// <summary>
   111	        /// Enables capture for disabled dates within the selected date range.
   112	        /// </summary>
   113	        /// <remarks>
   114	        /// By default, it will always ignore disabled dates. This parameter will take effect when <see cref="MudBaseDatePicker.IsDateDisabledFunc"/> is set.
   115	        /// </remarks>
   116	        [Parameter]
   117	        [Category(CategoryTypes.FormComponent.Validation)]
   118	        public bool AllowDisabledDatesInRange { get; set; } = false;
   119	
   120	        protected async Task SetDateRangeAsync(DateRange? range, bool updateValue)
   121	        {
   122	            // Normalize the DateRange before exception is thrown
   123	            range = NormalizeDateRange(range);
   124	
   125	            if (_dateRange != range)
   126	            {
   127	                var doesRangeContainDisabledDates = !AllowDisabledDatesInRange && range is { Start: not null, End: not null } && Enumerable
   128	                    .Range(0, int.MaxValue)
   129	                    .Select(index => range.Start.Value.AddDays(index))
   130	                    .TakeWhile(date => date <= range.End.Value)
   131	                    .Any(date => IsDateDisabledFunc(date.Date));
   132	
   133	                if (doesRangeContainDisabledDates)
   134	                {
   135	                    _rangeText = null;
   136	                    await SetTextAsync(null, false);
   137	                    return;
   138	                }
   139	
   140	                Touched = true;
   141	
   142	                if (range?.Start is not null && StartMonth == null)
   143	                    PickerMonth = new DateTime(GetCulture().Calendar.GetYear(range.Start.Value), GetCulture().Calendar.GetMonth(range.Start.Value), 1, GetCulture().Calendar);
   144	
   145	                _dateRange = range;
   146	                _value = range?.End;
   147	                HighlightedDate = range?.Start;
   148	
   149	                if (updateValue)
   150	                {
   151	                    ResetConverterErrors();
   152	                    if (_dateRange == null || (_dateRange.Start == null && _dateRange.End == null))
   153	                    {
   154	                        _rangeText = null;
   155	                        await SetTextAsync(null, false);
   156	                    }
   157	                    else
   158	                    {
   159	                        _rangeText = new Range<string>(
   160	                            ConvertSet(_dateRange.Start),
   161	                            ConvertSet(_dateRange.End));
   162	                        await SetTextAsync(_dateRange.ToString(GetConverter()), false);
   163	                    }
   164	                }
   165	
   166	                await DateRangeChanged.InvokeAsync(_dateRange);
   167	                await BeginValidateAsync();
   168	                FieldChanged(_value);
   169	            }
   170	        }
   171	
   172	        private Range<string>? RangeText
   173	        {
   174	            get => _rangeText;
   175	            set
   176	            {
   177	                if (_rangeText?.Equals(value) ?? (value == null))
   178	                    return;
   179	
   180	                Touched = true;
   181	                _rangeText = value;
   182	                SetDateRangeAsync(value is null ? null : ParseDateRangeValue(value.Start, value.End), false).CatchAndLog();
   183	            }
   184	        }
   185	
   186	        private MudRangeInput<string> _rangeInput = null!;
   187	
   188	        /// <summary>
   189	        /// Focuses the start input.
   190	        /// </summary>

   224	        protected override Task DateFormatChangedAsync(string? newFormat)
   225	        {
   226	            Touched = true;
   227	            _rangeText = null;
   228	            if (_dateRange?.Start != null || _dateRange?.End != null)
   229	            {
   230	                _rangeText = new Range<string>(
   231	                    ConvertSet(_dateRange.Start),
   232	                    ConvertSet(_dateRange.End));
   233	            }
   234	
   235	            return SetTextAsync(_dateRange?.ToString(GetConverter()), false);
   236	        }
   237	
   238	        protected override Task StringValueChangedAsync(string? value)
   239	        {
   240	            Touched = true;
   241	            // Update the date range property (without updating back the Value property)
   242	            return SetDateRangeAsync(ParseDateRangeValue(value), false);
   243	        }
   244	
   245	        protected override bool HasValue(DateTime? value) => value is not null;
   246	
   247	        protected override bool IsDayDisabled(DateTime date)
   248	        {
   249	            if (_firstDate is null || _secondDate is not null)
   250	            {
   251	                return base.IsDayDisabled(date);
   252	            }
   253	
   254	            var selectedDate = _firstDate.Value;
   255	            var validDateRange = GetValidDateRange(selectedDate);
   256	
   257	            return base.IsDayDisabled(date) || IsDateOutOfRange(date, selectedDate, validDateRange);
   258	        }
   259	
   260	        private DateRange GetValidDateRange(DateTime selectedDate)
   261	        {
   262	            var start = MinDays switch
   263	            {
   264	                null => MinDate ?? DateTime.MinValue,
   265	                _ when _allowDisabledDatesInCountState.Value => selectedDate.Date.AddDays(MinDays.Value - 1),
   266	                _ => _minValidDate
   267	            };
   268	
   269	            var end = MaxDays switch
   270	            {
   271	                null => MaxDate ?? DateTime.MaxValue,
   272	                _ when _allowDisabledDatesInCountState.Value => selectedDate.Date.AddDays(MaxDays.Value - 1),
   273	                _ => _maxValidDate
   274	            };
   275	
   276	            return new DateRange(start, end);
   277	        }
   278	
   279	        private static bool IsDateOutOfRange(DateTime date, DateTime selectedDate, DateRange validRange)
   280	        {
   281	            var isNotSelectedDate = date < selectedDate || date > selectedDate;
   282	            var isOutsideValidRange = date < validRange.Start || date > validRange.End;
   283	
   284	            return isNotSelectedDate && isOutsideValidRange;
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        private DateTime GetMaxSelectableDate(DateTime startDate, int maxDays)
   288	        {
   289	            var validDayCount = 1;
   290	            var lastValidDate = startDate;
   291	            var maxDate = startDate.AddDays(1);
   292	
   293	            while (validDayCount < maxDays)
   294	            {
   295	                if (!IsDateDisabledFunc(maxDate))
   296	                {
   297	                    validDayCount++;
   298	                    lastValidDate = maxDate;
   299	                }
   300	
   301	                if (validDayCount == maxDays)
   302	                    break;
   303	
   304	                if (maxDate.Date > MaxDate.GetValueOrDefault(startDate.AddYears(50)).Date)
   305	                    break;
   306	
   307	                if (maxDate.Date == DateTime.MaxValue.Date)
   308	                    break;
   309	
   310	                maxDate = maxDate.AddDays(1);
   311	            }
   312	
   313	            return lastValidDate;
   314	        }
   315	
   316	        /// <summary>
   317	        /// Recalculate the valid days in relation to the <see cref="MinDays"/> and <see cref="MaxDays"/> allowed
   318	        /// </summary>
   319	        public void RecalculateValidDays()
   320	        {
   321	            if (_firstDate is null) return;
   322	
   323	            if (MinDays is not null)
   324	                _minValidDate = GetMaxSelectableDate(_firstDate.Value, MinDays.Value);
   325	
   326	            if (MaxDays is not null)
   327	                _maxValidDate = GetMaxSelectableDate(_firstDate.Value, MaxDays.Value);
   328	
   329	            StateHasChanged();
   330	        }
   331	
   332	        private DateRange? ParseDateRangeValue(string? value)
   333	        {
   334	            return DateRange.TryParse(value, GetConverter(), out var dateRange) ? dateRange : null;
   335	        }
   336	
   337	        private DateRange? ParseDateRangeValue(string? start, string? end)
   338	        {
   339	            return DateRange.TryParse(start, end, GetConverter(), out var dateRange) ? dateRange : null;
   340	        }
   341	
   342	        protected override Task OnPickerClosedAsync()
   343	        {
   344	            _firstDate = null;
   345	
   346	            return base.OnPickerClosedAsync();
   347	        }
   348	
   349	        private bool CheckDateRange(DateTime day, Func<DateTime, DateTime, bool> compareStart, Func<DateTime, DateTime, bool> compareEnd)
   350	        {
   351	            return _firstDate is null
   352	                && _dateRange is { Start: { } start, End: { } end }
   353	                && compareStart(start.Date, day)
   354	                && compareEnd(end.Date, day);
   355	        }
   356	
   357	        protected override string GetDayClasses(int month, DateTime day)
   358	        {
   359	            var b = new CssBuilder("mud-day");
   360	            b.AddClass(AdditionalDateClassesFunc?.Invoke(day) ?? string.Empty);
   361	            if (day < GetMonthStart(month) || day > GetMonthEnd(month))
   362	            {
   363	                return b.AddClass("mud-hidden").Build();
   364	            }
   365	
   366	            static bool isLessThan(DateTime date1, DateTime date2) => date1 < date2;
   367	            static bool isGreaterThan(DateTime date1, DateTime date2) => date1 > date2;
   368	            static bool isEqualTo(DateTime date1, DateTime date2) => date1 == date2;
   369	            static bool isNotEqualTo(DateTime date1, DateTime date2) => date1 != date2;
   370	
   371	            if ((_firstDate?.Date < day && _secondDate?.Date > day) || CheckDateRange(day, compareStart: isLessThan, compareEnd: isGreaterThan))
   372	            {
   373	                return b
   374	                    .AddClass("mud-range")
   375	                    .AddClass("mud-range-between")
   376	                    .AddClass($"mud-current mud-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}-text mud-button-outlined mud-button-outlined-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}", day == DateTime.Today)
   377	                    .Build();
   378	            }
   379	
   380	            if (_firstDate?.Date == day && _secondDate?.Date == day)
   381	            {
   382	                return b.AddClass("mud-selected")
   383	                    .AddClass($"mud-theme-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}")
   384	                    .Build();
   385	            }
   386	
   387	            if (_firstDate?.Date == day || CheckDateRange(day, compareStart: isEqualTo, compareEnd: isNotEqualTo))
   388	            {
   389	                return b.AddClass("mud-selected")
   390	                    .AddClass("mud-range")
   391	                    .AddClass("mud-range-start-selected")
   392	                    .AddClass("mud-range-selection", _firstDate != null)
   393	                    .AddClass($"mud-theme-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}")
   394	                    .Build();
   395	            }
   396	
   397	            if ((_firstDate is { } && _secondDate?.Date == day) || CheckDateRange(day, compareStart: isNotEqualTo, compareEnd: isEqualTo))
   398	            {
   399	                return b.AddClass("mud-selected")
   400	                    .AddClass("mud-range")
   401	                    .AddClass("mud-range-end-selected")
   402	                    .AddClass($"mud-theme-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}")
   403	                    .Build();
   404	            }
   405	
   406	            if (CheckDateRange(day, compareStart: isEqualTo, compareEnd: isEqualTo))
   407	            {
   408	                return b.AddClass("mud-selected").AddClass($"mud-theme-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}").Build();
   409	            }
   410	
   411	            if (_firstDate?.Date < day)
   412	            {
   413	                return b.AddClass("mud-range", _secondDate is null && day != DateTime.Today)
   414	                    .AddClass("mud-range-selection")
   415	                    .AddClass($"mud-range-selection-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}", _firstDate is not null)
   416	                    .AddClass($"mud-current mud-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}-text mud-button-outlined mud-button-outlined-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}", day == DateTime.Today)
   417	                    .Build();
   418	            }
   419	
   420	            if (day == DateTime.Today)
   421	            {
   422	                return b.AddClass("mud-current")
   423	                    .AddClass($"mud-button-outlined mud-button-outlined-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}")
   424	                    .AddClass($"mud-{Color.ToStringFast(true)}-text")
   425	                    .Build();
   426	            }
   427	
   428	            return b.Build();
   429	        }
   430	
   431	        protected override async Task OnDayClickedAsync(DateTime dateTime)
   432	        {
   433	            if (GetReadOnlyState())
   434	                return;
   435	            if (_firstDate == null || _secondDate != null)
   436	            {
   437	                _secondDate = null;
   438	                _firstDate = dateTime;
   439	
   440	                RecalculateValidDays();
   441	
   442	                return;
   443	            }
   444	            if (_firstDate > dateTime)
   445	            {
   446	                _secondDate = _firstDate;
   447	                _firstDate = dateTime;
   448	            }
   449	            else
   450	            {
   451	                _secondDate = dateTime;
   452	            }
   453	            if (PickerActions == null || AutoClose)
   454	            {
   455	                await SubmitAsync();
   456	
   457	                if (PickerVariant != PickerVariant.Static)
   458	                {
   459	                    await Task.Delay(TimeSpan.FromMilliseconds(ClosingDelay), TimeProvider);
   460	                    await CloseAsync(false);
   461	                }
   462	            }
   463	        }
   464	
   465	        protected override Task OnOpenedAsync()
   466	        {
   467	            _secondDate = null;
   468	            return base.OnOpenedAsync();
   469	        }
   470	
   471	        protected internal override async Task SubmitAsync()
   472	        {
   473	            if (GetReadOnlyState())
   474	                return;
   475	            if (_firstDate == null || _secondDate == null)
   476	                return;
   477	
   478	            await SetDateRangeAsync(new DateRange(_firstDate, _secondDate), true);
   479	
   480	            _firstDate = null;
   481	            _secondDate = null;
   482	        }
   483	
   484	        protected override Task ResetValueAsync() => ClearAsync();
   485	
   486	        public override async Task ClearAsync(bool close = true)
   487	        {
   488	            await SetDateRangeAsync(null, true);
   489	            _firstDate = _secondDate = null;
   490	            await base.ClearAsync(close);
   491	        }
   492	
   493	        protected override string GetTitleDateString()
   494	        {
   495	            if (_firstDate != null)
   496	                return $"{FormatTitleDate(_firstDate)} - {FormatTitleDate(_secondDate)}";
   497	
   498	            return DateRange?.Start != null
   499	                ? $"{FormatTitleDate(DateRange.Start)} - {FormatTitleDate(DateRange.End)}"
   500	                : "";
   501	        }
   502	
   503	        protected override DateTime GetCalendarStartOfMonth()
   504	        {
   505	            var date = StartMonth ?? DateRange?.Start ?? DateTime.Today;
   506	            return date.StartOfMonth(GetCulture());
   507	        }
   508	
   509	        protected override async Task OnYearClickedAsync(int year)
   510	        {
   511	            await base.OnYearClickedAsync(year);
   512	
   513	            if (DateRange?.Start is null && _firstDate is null)
   514	            {
   515	                HighlightedDate = PickerMonth;
   516	            }
   517	        }
   518	
   519	        protected override int GetCalendarYear(DateTime yearDate)
   520	        {
   521	            var date = DateRange?.Start ?? DateTime.Today;
   522	            var diff = GetCulture().Calendar.GetYear(date) - GetCulture().Calendar.GetYear(yearDate);
   523	            var calenderYear = GetCulture().Calendar.GetYear(date);
   524	            return calenderYear - diff;
   525	        }
   526	
   527	        /// <summary>
   528	        /// Normalize a date by treating DateTime.MinValue as null
   529	        /// This prevents an ArgumentOutOfRangeException from happening when performing date arithmetic
   530	        /// </summary>
   531	        /// <param name="date">The date to normalize</param>
   532	        /// <returns>Normalized date or null</returns>
   533	        private static DateTime? NormalizeDate(DateTime? date)
   534	        {
   535	            if (date is null)
   536	                return null;
   537	
   538	            // Treat DateTime.MinValue as null
   539	            if (date.Value == DateTime.MinValue)
   540	                return null;
   541	
   542	            return date;
   543	        }
   544	
   545	        /// <summary>
   546	        /// Normalize a date range by checking the start date and end date for DateTime.MinValue
   547	        /// This prevents an ArgumentOutOfRangeException from happening when performing date arithmetic
   548	        /// </summary>
   549	        /// <see cref="NormalizeDate"/>
   550	        /// <param name="range">The date range to normalize</param>
   551	        /// <returns>Normalized date range or null</returns>
   552	        private static DateRange? NormalizeDateRange(DateRange? range)
   553	        {
   554	            if (range is null)
   555	                return null;
   556	
   557	            var start = NormalizeDate(range.Start);
   558	            var end = NormalizeDate(range.End);
   559	
   560	            return new DateRange(start, end);
   561	        }
   562	
   563	    }
   564	}

2026-05-29 13:30:21,783 - INFO - swea-agent-MudBlazor__MudBlazor-12973 - 💭 THOUGHT
Now, the issue is that when `StartInputAriaLabel` is null on `MudDateRangePicker`, we want the default to be "Start date" (from `LanguageResource.MudDateRangePicker_Start`), not "Start" (from `LanguageResource.MudRangeInput_Start`). 

The way the MudRangeInput works, it uses:
```
aria-label="@(StartInputAriaLabel ?? Localizer[LanguageResource.MudRangeInput_Start])"
```

So if we pass `StartInputAriaLabel="@StartInputAriaLabel"` from MudDateRangePicker, and `StartInputAriaLabel` is null, then MudRangeInput will use its own default which is "Start". 

To change this behavior, we need the MudDateRangePicker to pass its own default. We can do this by adding an injected Localizer in MudDateRangePicker.razor and passing the appropriate default:

Let me check if MudDateRangePicker has access to a Localizer. Looking at the pattern in MudRangeInput.razor:
```
@inject InternalMudLocalizer Localizer
```

We can do the same in MudDateRangePicker.razor. But wait, MudDateRangePicker.razor inherits from MudBaseDatePicker which likely already has access to this.

Actually, looking more carefully at the MudDateRangePicker.razor, I need to update it to pass the localized defaults. Let me update it:







🎬 ACTION
cat > /testbed/src/MudBlazor/Components/DatePicker/MudDateRangePicker.razor << 'EOF'
﻿@namespace MudBlazor
@using MudBlazor.Resources
@inherits MudBaseDatePicker
@inject InternalMudLocalizer Localizer

@Render

@code{

    protected override RenderFragment InputContent=>
        @<MudInputControl Label="@Label" Variant="@Variant" HelperText="@HelperText" Error="@ErrorState.Value"
                          ErrorText="@ErrorTextState.Value" Disabled="@GetDisabledState()" Margin="@Margin" Required="@Required"
                          @onclick="async () => { if (!Editable) await ToggleStateAsync(); }" ForId="@FieldId">
               <InputContent>
                   <MudRangeInput @ref="_rangeInput"
                                  @attributes="UserAttributes"
                                  InputType="@InputType.Text"
                                  Class="@PickerInputClassname"
                                  Style="@Style"
                                  Variant="@Variant"
                                  ReadOnly="@(!Editable)"
                                  Label="@Label"
                                  @bind-Value="@RangeText"
                                  Disabled="@GetDisabledState()"
                                  Adornment="@Adornment"
                                  AdornmentIcon="@AdornmentIcon"
                                  AdornmentColor="@AdornmentColor"
                                  IconSize="@IconSize"
                                  OnAdornmentClick="ToggleStateAsync"
                                  Required="@Required"
                                  RequiredError="@RequiredError"
                                  Error="@ErrorState.Value"
                                  ErrorText="@ErrorTextState.Value"
                                  Margin="@Margin"

                                  PlaceholderEnd="@PlaceholderEnd"

                                  EndInputAriaLabel="@(EndInputAriaLabel ?? Localizer[LanguageResource.MudDateRangePicker_End])"
                                  Clearable="@(Clearable && !GetReadOnlyState())"
                                  ClearIcon="@ClearIcon"
                                  Underline="@Underline"

     1	﻿using Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection;
     2	using Microsoft.Extensions.Localization;
     3	
     4	namespace MudBlazor;
     5	
     6	/// <summary>
     7	/// Internal localization entry point that delegates translation work to configured interceptors.
     8	/// </summary>
     9	/// <remarks>
    10	/// Components access localization through this class so they can be decoupled from specific resource providers. By default it uses <see cref="DefaultLocalizationInterceptor"/>, but applications can plug in custom interceptors.
    11	/// </remarks>
    12	internal sealed class InternalMudLocalizer
    13	{
    14	    private readonly ILocalizationInterceptor _interceptor;
    15	    private readonly ILocalizationEnumInterceptor _enumInterceptor;
    16	
    17	    /// <summary>
    18	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="InternalMudLocalizer"/> class.
    19	    /// </summary>
    20	    /// <param name="interceptor">The localization interceptor to use for handling translations.</param>
    21	    public InternalMudLocalizer(ILocalizationInterceptor interceptor)
    22	        : this(interceptor, new DefaultLocalizationEnumInterceptor(interceptor))
    23	    {
    24	    }
    25	
    26	    /// <summary>
    27	    /// Initializes a new instance of the <see cref="InternalMudLocalizer"/> class.
    28	    /// </summary>
    29	    /// <param name="interceptor">The localization interceptor to use for handling translations.</param>
    30	    /// <param name="enumInterceptor">The localization interceptor to use for handling enumeration translations.</param>
    31	    [ActivatorUtilitiesConstructor]
    32	    public InternalMudLocalizer(ILocalizationInterceptor interceptor, ILocalizationEnumInterceptor enumInterceptor)
    33	    {
    34	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(interceptor);
    35	        ArgumentNullException.ThrowIfNull(enumInterceptor);
    36	
    37	        _interceptor = interceptor;
    38	        _enumInterceptor = enumInterceptor;
    39	    }
    40	
    41	    /// <summary>
    42	    /// Gets the string resource with the given name.
    43	    /// </summary>
    44	    /// <param name="key">The name of the string resource.</param>
    45	    /// <param name="arguments">The list of arguments to be passed to the string resource.</param>
    46	    /// <returns>The string resource as a <see cref="LocalizedString" />.</returns>
    47	    public LocalizedString this[string key, params object[] arguments] => _interceptor.Handle(key, arguments);
    48	
    49	    /// <summary>
    50	    /// Localizes the specified enumeration value.
    51	    /// </summary>
    52	    /// <param name="enumeration">The enumeration value to be localized.</param>
    53	    /// <returns>The localized representation of the enumeration value.</returns>
    54	    public string this[Enum enumeration] => _enumInterceptor.Handle(enumeration);
    55	}

Now let me verify the complete flow one more time:

1. `MudRangeInput` has `StartInputAriaLabel` and `EndInputAriaLabel` properties.
